\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\begin{DoxyVerb}A terminal style.

A terminal style consists of a color (`color`), a background color (`bgcolor`), and a number of attributes, such
as bold, italic etc. The attributes have 3 states: they can either be on
(``True``), off (``False``), or not set (``None``).

Args:
    color (Union[Color, str], optional): Color of terminal text. Defaults to None.
    bgcolor (Union[Color, str], optional): Color of terminal background. Defaults to None.
    bold (bool, optional): Enable bold text. Defaults to None.
    dim (bool, optional): Enable dim text. Defaults to None.
    italic (bool, optional): Enable italic text. Defaults to None.
    underline (bool, optional): Enable underlined text. Defaults to None.
    blink (bool, optional): Enabled blinking text. Defaults to None.
    blink2 (bool, optional): Enable fast blinking text. Defaults to None.
    reverse (bool, optional): Enabled reverse text. Defaults to None.
    conceal (bool, optional): Enable concealed text. Defaults to None.
    strike (bool, optional): Enable strikethrough text. Defaults to None.
    underline2 (bool, optional): Enable doubly underlined text. Defaults to None.
    frame (bool, optional): Enable framed text. Defaults to None.
    encircle (bool, optional): Enable encircled text. Defaults to None.
    overline (bool, optional): Enable overlined text. Defaults to None.
    link (str, link): Link URL. Defaults to None.
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{pip_2__vendor_2rich_2style_8py_source_l00031}{31}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{pip_2__vendor_2rich_2style_8py_source}{style.\+py}}.

 str pip.\+\_\+vendor.\+rich.\+style.\+Style.\+render (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{str }]{text}{ = {\ttfamily "{}"{}}, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{}{, }\item[{Optional\mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classpip_1_1__vendor_1_1rich_1_1color_1_1ColorSystem}{Color\+System}}\mbox{]} }]{color\+\_\+system}{ = {\ttfamily ColorSystem.TRUECOLOR}, }\item[{bool }]{legacy\+\_\+windows}{ = {\ttfamily False}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Render the ANSI codes for the style.

Args:
    text (str, optional): A string to style. Defaults to "".
    color_system (Optional[ColorSystem], optional): Color system to render to. Defaults to ColorSystem.TRUECOLOR.

Returns:
    str: A string containing ANSI style codes.
\end{DoxyVerb}
